<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
The staff at Pacific Veterinary Hospital are excellent. They are professional, competent, caring, and friendly. They helped us with cremation of our first dog after we moved to the neighborhood. When my second dog became ill, they worked hard to figure out treatment options, and worked to make his medication affordable. He lived for an additional 7 years after becoming ill, and they get a lot of credit for that. They are reasonably priced, and also provided expert consultation at no additional charge. Now they provide all the routine care for our third dog. Their rates are generally about 50% to 30% below other vets I have tried in the past.</Text>

After searching around, I found Iron Orr Fitness, and I explained my situation to them through the form they have on their website. Within the next business day, I got a reply back and was given a complimentary session with Brett Wheeless to assess my goals, my strengths, weaknesses, and everything else.

Jump forward to right now, and I am still with Iron Orr and am going to stick with Brett for as long as I possibly can.

Brett has been nothing short of an excellent trainer. In our first few sessions together, he has done everything to fix so much of my technique on all 4 of the major lifts, including:

- Strengthening my glutes and stretching/strengthening out my hip muscles (to fix my hip alignment that was causing me to have a functional leg length discrepancy)
- Fixing my deadlift form so that I do not hurt my lower back on heavier weights
- Fixing my bench press form to ensure that I never tear my rotator cuffs
- Adjusting my overhead press form so that I get more shoulder activation and ensuring that my lower back is in a safe position on every rep
- And much, much more...

Where has he been all my life? With his amazing guidance and support, my numbers on my lifts are going up now, and I no longer feel the discomforts that I've had in my lifts from years prior. He's just really good at what he does, and I can't thank him enough.

If ever you need to find a personal trainer to help your powerlifting that is not only intelligent in the personal training field but is also a great man to talk to about anything at all, Brett Wheeless is your man. He will get you your results. In fact, I recommend him to everyone, regardless of your goals.<//text>

This gym is pretty well stocked for being in a relatively small space, it has everything you need and more.

They have the standard things:
Free weights, bench press and incline press racks, squat and deadlift stations, treadmills, all the machines you could need.

They also have many extras:

< review>
I was introduced to Afterburn by a school friend that had done the three person challenge. At first, I was only going to do the online version of this most recent challenge, however, I know myself and knew that if I didn't workout there I wouldn't get the results I wanted. Going in for the first class at 4 in the morning, I was more than intimidated. Little did I know that I was walking into the most supportive, motivating, and inspirational gym. Sure, all of the amazing trainers were welcoming and more than willing to help, but what made it was the people working out next to me. People would tell me, "Keep going" or "You're doing awesome!" I love Afterburn because you can really measure your results; going from not being able to do 1 burpee, to doing 130 in Dave's MMA class was a huge accomplishment for me. I ended up finishing 87 out of about 600 people in the challenge, losing 19 pounds and just over 6% body fat. This place is unbelievable!!!</review>

<Date>1518276843019<//Date><rate>5<//rate><Text>AWESOME place to work out!!

Did Crossfit in grad school, then work life happened in a startup, tons of travels, kid..took a break and following a few unsuccessful attempts the local AfterBurn made the comeback easy again: classes on YOUR skill level (ramp up to 60 minutes of "why did I choose to get my butt kicked?"), COACHES who actually coach (check the on ramp class, awesome for beginners and those who care about proper form before number of reps which comes automatically) and way more!

All in all excellent setup that was even convinincing to friends and family to start their crossfit experience.

Sometimes it's bring able to take the initial baby steps that get you to love core and eventually fit45, aka 45 minutes of "let's prep for Hollywood's next Gladiator movie".

Oh, last point: they offer child care. All you hip millenials won't care too much yet but guess what, you too will multiply or procreate and then wonder where time went to work out! This Childcare option allows you to take your gal/guy that you met in better shape a couple of years ago and get back to that shape as kiddo is happy on the second floor with other kids while you're sweating your A$$ off, building your AB$. Fun times as I said.

<Rating>4<//Rating><Review>I was a member here for about a year I was coming from Golds Gym, I say that to preface my next comments as I may have been a little spoiled, It isn't really fair to compare a gym like Golds to Afterburn...But in this case ill do it anyway.

Pros:
Afterbum Fitness offers a variety of very challenging classes for whatever your fitness goals maybe, which is really good if you want isolated attention and you don't want to pay for a personal trainer, the classes will offer you personal training in a group setting. Afterburn offers child care at an additional cost which was fantastic for me personally, the ladies where nice and responsible while making me feel comfortable leaving my little man in there temporary care. Additionally they have a nice Juice Bar with a variety of delicious selections, the staff is nice and will do what it takes to meet your needs for the most part. Afterburn additionally has an app for scheduling classes and to view your account information which was/is very useful and the treadmills are TOP NOTCH...all fantastic things about the gym.

Cons:
The Facilities overall are mediocre at least considering the price of things, The mens restroom/locker area is a little on the smelly end of things and often lacks toilet paper for whatever reason...but it is ALWAYS CLEAN in appearance, the workout machines and such are "ok" they are slightly dated, showing that they are not necessarily a priority considering 80 percent of the members take classes and my not be using the weight lifting equipment.

So with that being said it comes down to what you like if you are a little more on the self motivated end of things (like to stick to a regime and can stay motivated with that independently) then Afterburn may NOT be for you especially considering the price is over 100 dollars and around 40 additional dollars if you include childcare....But if you like a group setting and really interesting workouts then Afterburn is YOUR place it will keep you interested and motivated...<//Review><pictures>None<//pictures><Response>{'time': 1435421061541, 'text': 'Charles,\n\nThanks for the review and all the great things said! < review>
I've brought all my dry cleaning to Magic Touch for the past 4 years.  The primary reason I've gone there is convenience.  It's located right next door to where I live.  In general, my experience has been pretty decent.  It's a bit pricey, but they have a pretty quick turn around and are generally friendly.

I had an issue a few months back where they lost a shirt of mine.  That was frustrating, but they gave me a credit for the value of the shirt.

The situation that bothered me most, resulting in this one star review, occurred just recently.  I brought in a large bunch of shirts (20 or so).  When I got them back, I noticed that two of them (back to back in the bag) had stains that were in the shape of buttons next to the button holes the whole way down the shirts.  It looks like buttons were pressed against the shirt and melted a bit, leaving a glossy plastic residue (see photos).

I brought the shirts back in.  The owner said she'd try to fix them.  When I went back to pick them up, the owner explained that she wasn't able to get the stains out.  She denied responsibility for the damage stating that she doesn't have any equipment that could have caused those marks.  I told her that the shirts were fine when I dropped them off, but she insisted that she couldn't have caused that damage and suggested that I must have done something to them.

It's incredibly frustrating to be told that I'm to blame for this damage, when it's so obvious that they did something to them to cause this, especially since I've been a customer for years. I eventually told her I'd be taking my business elsewhere in the future.

I've tried to get the stains out on my own with no success.  Both are ruined and one of them was a custom shirt I got while in Thailand, so it's not easily replaceable.

My real issue is their complete denial of responsibility for ruining my clothes, then blaming me.< /review>
